document.createTextNode(\'R\xc3\xa9serv\xc3\xa9s aux administrateurs\');\n      titleElem.appendChild(titleTxt);\n\n      adminNav.appendChild(titleElem);\n\n\n      // buttons\n      var adminButtons = [{\n        text: \'Annuaire\',\n        href: libeUserInfo.url_dock + \'/annuaire/\',\n      },{\n        text: \'Back office\',\n        href: libeUserInfo.url_quai + \'/quai/\',\n      },{\n        text: \'\xc3\x89diter\',\n        href: "javascript:location.href = \'"+ libeUserInfo.url_quai +"/quai/redirect_to_change_view?u=\' + location.href;",\n      },{\n        text: \'Actualiser\',\n        href: "javascript: window.location.href = window.location.pathname + \'?refresh=\' + Math.floor((Math.random() * 1000000) + 1);",\n      }];\n\n      if (libeUserInfo.is_superuser && typeof(objectId) !== \'undefined\') {\n        adminButtons.push({\n          text: \'Compose\',\n          href: libeUserInfo.url_dock + \'/compose/\' + objectId + \'/\'\n        })\n      }\n\n      for (i = 0; i < adminButtons.length; i++) {\n        var elem = document.createElement(\'a\');\n        elem.href = adminButtons[i][\'href\'];\n        var txt = document.createTextNode(adminButtons[i][\'text\']);\n        elem.appendChild(txt);\n        adminNav.appendChild(elem);\n      }\n\n      headerElem.insertBefore(adminNav, headerElem.firstChild);\n      headerFixNavHeight = headerElem.offsetHeight;\n      document.body.style.paddingTop = headerFixNavHeight + \'px\';\n    }\n  }\n  if (libeUserInfo.access_level !== \'PRE\' ) {\n      var advertisement_script = document.createElement(\'script\');\n      advertisement_script.setAttribute(\'src\',"https://statics.liberation.fr/newsite/js/advertisement.js");\n      document.head.appendChild(advertisement_script);\n  }\n</script>\n\n\n\n</div>\n\n\n  <script type="text/javascript">\n    if (libeUserInfo.access_level === \'PRE\') {\n      setCookie("n0d", 1);\n      var navUserLabel = document.getElementsByClassName(\'js-nav-label\')[0];\n      navUserLabel.innerText = "\xc3\x89dition abonn\xc3\xa9";\n    } else { setCookie("n0d", "", "",-1); }\n  </script>\n\n\n    \n      \n    \n\n    \n  \n\n\n\n\n\n<main id="main-content" class="main-content main-page-home">\n  <div class="width-wrap clearfix">\n    <div class="home-pub-container
